*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) {\n\tc.namespacePoliciesMutex.Lock()\n\tdefer c.namespacePoliciesMutex.Unlock()\n\n\tns := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tc.namespacePolicyCounts[ns]++\n\n\tc.log.DebugContext(\n\t\tcontext.Background(),\n\t\t\"Policy upserted\",\n\t\tlogfields.Namespace, ns,\n\t\tlogfields.Name, policy.GetName(),\n\t\t\"policyCount\", c.namespacePolicyCounts[ns],\n\t)\n}\n\n// handlePolicyDelete processes a deleted CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (c *PolicyQuotaController) ns,\n\t\tlogfields.Name, policy.GetName(),\n\t\t\"policyCount\", c.namespacePolicyCounts[ns],\n\t)\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if the given namespace is within its policy quota.\n// It returns an error Delete one policy\n\tcontroller.handlePolicyDelete(policy1)\n\n\t// Should now be within quota\n\terr = controller.CheckQuota(\"default\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Verify count decreased\n\trequire.Equal(t, 1, controller.GetNamespacePolicyCount(\"default\"))\n}\n\nfunc TestPolicyQuotaController_GetNamespacePolicyCount(t *testing.T) {\n\tlog := slog.Default()\n\tmockRes :=
